<body>

<div style="font-family:Helvetica;">

<p align="right" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit 99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Apple Reports
Fourth Quarter Results</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Revenues increase by 19 percent</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">CUPERTINO, California&#151;October 15, 2003&#151;Apple&#174; today announced
financial results for its fiscal 2003 fourth quarter ended September 27, 2003.
For the quarter, the Company posted a net profit of $44 million, or $.12 per
diluted share. These results compare to a net loss of $45 million, or $.13 per
diluted share, in the year-ago quarter. Revenues for the quarter were $1.715
billion, up 19 percent from the year-ago quarter, and gross margins were 26.6
percent, up from 26.4 percent in the year-ago quarter. International sales
accounted for 38 percent of the quarter&#146;s revenues.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">The quarter&#146;s results include an after-tax investment gain of
$6 million, a favorable accounting transition adjustment of $3 million related
to Apple&#146;s stock repurchase agreement, and a gain on settlement of the stock
repurchase agreement of $6 million.&#160;
Without these items, net income would have been $29 million, or $.08 per
share.&#160; Management believes that
presentation of results excluding these items provides meaningful supplemental
information regarding the Company&#146;s operational performance.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple shipped 787 thousand Macintosh&#174; units during the
quarter, up 7% from the year-ago quarter, as well as 336 thousand iPod</font><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-family:Symbol;font-size:10.0pt;">&#210;</font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;"> units, up 140% from the
year-ago quarter.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;It was a great new product quarter for Apple,&#148; said Steve
Jobs, Apple&#146;s CEO. &#147;We launched the Power Mac G5, the fastest personal computer
in the world, new PowerBooks and new iPods.&#160;
Plus, we&#146;re delivering Panther, the next major release of Mac OS X,
later this month and we&#146;ll have some exciting news regarding our music efforts
tomorrow.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;We are very pleased to have exceeded our revenue and profit
targets for the fourth quarter,&#148; said Fred Anderson, Apple&#146;s CFO. &#147;Our balance
sheet remains strong and our working capital management is among the best in
the industry.&#160; Looking ahead to the
first quarter of fiscal 2004, we expect a sequential increase in revenues to
about $1.9 billion and a slight sequential increase in GAAP earnings relative
to the September quarter.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">For the year, the Company reported net income of $69 million
on revenues of $6.21 billion compared to net income of $65 million on revenues
of $5.74 billion in 2002.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple ignited the personal computer revolution in the 1970s
with the Apple II and reinvented the personal computer in the 1980s with the
Macintosh. Apple is committed to bringing the best personal computing
experience to students, educators, creative professionals and consumers around
the world through its innovative hardware, software and Internet offerings.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Apple will provide live streaming of its Q4 2003 financial
results conference call utilizing QuickTime&#153;, Apple&#146;s standards-based
technology for live and on-demand audio and video streaming. The live webcast
will begin at 2:30 p.m. PT on Wednesday, October 15, 2003 at
http://www.apple.com/quicktime/qtv/earningsq403/ and will also be available for
replay. The QuickTime player is available free for Macintosh and Windows users
at www.apple.com/quicktime.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">This
press release contains forward-looking statements about future revenues,
profit, and products, including statements regarding delivery of Mac OS</font><font size="2" color="black" face="Symbol" style="color:windowtext;font-family:Symbol;font-size:10.0pt;">&#210;</font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;"> X version 10.3
&quot;Panther,&quot; </font><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">announcements</font><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;"> regarding the Company's music
efforts and estimated revenues and earnings for the first quarter of fiscal
2004.&#160; These statements involve risks
and uncertainties and actual results may differ. Potential risks and
uncertainties include continued competitive pressures in the marketplace; the effect
competitive and economic factors and the Company&#146;s reaction to them may have on
consumer and business buying decisions with respect to the Company&#146;s products;
the ability of the Company to make timely delivery of new programs, products
and successful technological innovations to the marketplace; the continued
availability of certain components and services essential to the Company&#146;s
business currently obtained by the Company from sole or limited sources;
possible disruption in commercial activities caused by terrorist activity and
armed conflict, such as changes in logistics and security arrangements, and</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<div style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
</font>

<p align="center" style="color:black;font-size:12.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">reduced end-user purchases relative to expectations; possible
disruption in commercial activity as a result of major health concerns, such as
Severe Acute Respiratory Syndrome (SARS); risks associated with the Company&#146;s
retail initiative including significant investment cost, uncertain consumer
acceptance and potential impact on existing reseller relationships; the effect
that the Company&#146;s dependency on manufacturing and logistics services provided
by third-parties may have on the quality or quantity of products manufactured;
and the ability of the Company to successfully evolve its operating system and
attract sufficient Macintosh developers. More information on potential factors
that could affect the Company&#146;s financial results is included from time to time
in the Company&#146;s public reports filed with the SEC, including the Company&#146;s
Form 10-Q for the quarter ended June 28, 2003 and the Company&#146;s Form 10-K for
the 2003 fiscal year to be filed with the SEC.&#160;
The Company assumes no obligation to update any forward-looking
statements or information, which speak as of their respective dates.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Press Contact:</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Investor Relations Contacts:</font></p>

<p style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">NOTE TO EDITORS: For additional information visit Apple&#146;s PR

<p align="center" style="color:black;font-size:12.0pt;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;">&nbsp;</p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CONSOLIDATED BALANCE SHEETS</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-autospace:none;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

Services have been reclassified from Other Segments to the Americas segment to
conform to the Q4&#146;03 presentation.</p>
